***дешевизна.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дешевизна.html>дешеви́зна</a> (25554)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевый.html>дешёвый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dešóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-изна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-izna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевизна.html>дешеви́зна</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">deševízna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевизна.html>дешеви́зны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевизна.html>дешеви́зны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевизна.html>дешеви́зн</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cheapness</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Often stressed as <i><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевизна.html>дешевизна́</a></i>, which is not recognized by dictionaries.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ше<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ви́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>з<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дешев-</b>; суффикс: <b>-изн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***дешевка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дешевка.html>дешёвка</a> (14445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевый.html>дешёвый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dešóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевка.html>дешёвка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dešóvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевка.html>дешёвки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевка.html>дешёвки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевка.html>дешёвок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> low price
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дешевка.html>дешёвке</a></i></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i>kupitʹ po dešóvke</i></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to buy cheap</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a cheap, worthless thing; cheapie</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шёв<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i>малодушный, <a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожный.html>ничто́жный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевка.html>дешёвку</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевка.html>дешёвок</a></i>).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дешёв-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-к</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***дешевый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дешевый.html>дешёвый</a> (2337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дешевъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deševŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*deševъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевый.html>дешёвый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dešóvyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)деше́вле</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дешеве́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дешеве́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дешеве́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cheap, empty, worthless
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевый.html>дешёвом</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:электрический.html>электри́ческом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рай.html>раю́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V <b>dešóvom</b> elektríčeskom rajú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">In a cheap electrical heaven</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cheap, inexpensive, low (of a price)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевый.html>дешёвые</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Cény tam <b>dešóvyje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">The prices over there are low.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположенный.html>располо́женная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мых</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевый.html>дешёвых</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:район.html>райо́нов</a> москвы́</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">raspolóžennaja v odnóm iz sámyx <b>dešóvyx</b> rajónov Moskvý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">situated in one of the very cheapest districts of Moscow</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The comparative <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">деше́вле</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dešévle</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used in the literal meaning of "inexpensive", while <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дешеве́е</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deševéje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used in figurative meanings.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевизна.html>дешеви́зна</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">deševízna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дешевка.html>дешёвка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dešóvka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шё<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a/c-ё. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>деше́вле </i><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a><i> подеше́вле </i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>цены</a>)<i>, дешеве́е </i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> перен. знач.)<i>.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дешёв-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деяние.html>дея́ние</a> (10770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">де́ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деяние.html>дея́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dejánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деяние.html>дея́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деяние.html>дея́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деяние.html>дея́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deed, act, action, exploit (heroic or extraordinary deed)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:джинн.html>джинн</a> (11061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">جِنّ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jinn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:джинн.html>джинн</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">džinn</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:джинн.html>джи́нна</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:джинн.html>джи́нны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:джинн.html>джи́ннов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>jinn, jinni, genie <i>(any of a class of spirits from Islamic mythology)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:диагностический.html>диагности́ческий</a> (17469)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диагностика.html>диагно́стика</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">diagnóstika</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">diagnostics, diagnosis</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-eskij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ish, -ic</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диагностический.html>диагности́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">diagnostíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>diagnostic</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:диаграмма.html>диагра́мма</a> (19061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диаграмма.html>диагра́мма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">diagrámma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диаграмма.html>диагра́ммы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диаграмма.html>диагра́ммы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диаграмма.html>диагра́мм</a></b>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ди.html>ди</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>гра́м<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ма</b>
